```typescript
Body: { title, content, category }
Response: { success: true, post: Post }

// 5. ê²Œì‹œê¸€ ì‚­ì œ
DELETE /api/posts/:id
Response: { success: true }
```

## ğŸ’¡ í–¥í›„ ê°œì„  ì‚¬í•­

### 1. ë™ì  IP ê°ì§€

### 2. ë„¤íŠ¸ì›Œí¬ ìƒíƒœ í™•ì¸
```typescript

// ë„¤íŠ¸ì›Œí¬ ì—°ê²° ìƒíƒœ í™•ì¸

  const state = await NetInfo.fetch();
  if (!state.isConnected) {
    Alert.alert('ì˜¤ë¥˜', 'ì¸í„°ë„· ì—°ê²°ì„ í™•ì¸í•´ì£¼ì„¸ìš”.');
```

### 3. ìë™ ì¬ì‹œë„ ë¡œì§
```typescript
const retryRequest = async (fn, retries = 3) => {
  for (let i = 0; i < retries; i++) {
    try {
      return await fn();
    } catch (error) {
      if (i === retries - 1) throw error;
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000 * (i + 1)));
    }
  }
};
```

```javascript
const isSameDay = (date1, date2) => {
  if (!date1 || !date2) return false;
  const d1 = new Date(date1);
  const d2 = new Date(date2);
  return d1.getFullYear() === d2.getFullYear() &&
         d1.getMonth() === d2.getMonth() &&
         d1.getDate() === d2.getDate();
};
```

### 1. ProgressSlider ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ ìƒì„± âœ…

**íŒŒì¼**: `mobile/components/ProgressSlider.js` (ì‹ ê·œ)

**ê¸°ëŠ¥**:
- ìŠ¬ë¼ì´ë”ë¡œ í•™ìŠµ ì§„í–‰ë„ ì¡°ì ˆ (0-100%, 5% ë‹¨ìœ„)
- ìë™ ì €ì¥ (5% ì´ìƒ ë³€ê²½ ì‹œ)
- ìƒíƒœ ìë™ ì „í™˜ í‘œì‹œ:
  - `interested` (ê´€ì‹¬ìˆìŒ) - íšŒìƒ‰
  - `learning` (í•™ìŠµì¤‘) - íŒŒë€ìƒ‰
  - `completed` (ì™„ë£Œ) - ì´ˆë¡ìƒ‰
- ì™„ë£Œ ì‹œ ì¶•í•˜ ë°°ì§€ í‘œì‹œ
- ë¡œë”© ì¸ë””ì¼€ì´í„° (ì €ì¥ ì¤‘)

**í•µì‹¬ ì½”ë“œ**:
```javascript
const handleProgressChange = async (value) => {
  const roundedValue = Math.round(value);
  setProgress(roundedValue);

  if (Math.abs(roundedValue - lastSavedProgress) >= 5) {
    try {
      setSaving(true);
      const response = await updateHobbyProgressAPI(hobbyId, roundedValue);
      setStatus(response.userHobby.status);
      setLastSavedProgress(roundedValue);
      if (onProgressChange) onProgressChange(response.userHobby);
    } catch (error) {
      setProgress(lastSavedProgress); // Revert on error
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  }
};
```

**íŒ¨í‚¤ì§€ ì„¤ì¹˜**:
```bash
npm install @react-native-community/slider
```

### 3. AddReviewModal ìˆ˜ì • ëª¨ë“œ ì§€ì› âœ…

**íŒŒì¼**: `mobile/components/AddReviewModal.js`

**ë³€ê²½ì‚¬í•­**:

```javascript
  hobbyName={hobby?.name}
```

```javascript
  if (editingSchedule) {
    // ISO ë‚ ì§œë¥¼ YYYY-MM-DD í˜•ì‹ìœ¼ë¡œ ë³€í™˜

```

## ğŸ¯ êµ¬í˜„ëœ ì£¼ìš” íŒ¨í„´

### 1. Edit Mode Pattern (ìˆ˜ì • ëª¨ë“œ íŒ¨í„´)
```javascript
// Modal ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸
const isEditMode = !!editingItem;

useEffect(() => {
  if (editingItem) {
    // Load existing data
    setField1(editingItem.field1);
    setField2(editingItem.field2);
  } else {
    // Reset for new
    resetForm();
  }
}, [editingItem, visible]);

// Submit handler
if (isEditMode) {
  await updateAPI(editingItem.id, data);
} else {
  await createAPI(data);
}
```

### 2. Inline Edit Pattern (ì¸ë¼ì¸ ìˆ˜ì • íŒ¨í„´)
```javascript
const [editingId, setEditingId] = useState(null);
const [editingText, setEditingText] = useState('');

{editingId === item.id ? (
  <EditView>
    <TextInput value={editingText} onChange={setEditingText} />
    <Button onPress={() => saveEdit(item.id)} />
  </EditView>
) : (
  <DisplayView>
    <Text>{item.content}</Text>
  </DisplayView>
)}
```

### 3. Long Press Pattern (ê¸¸ê²Œ ëˆ„ë¥´ê¸° íŒ¨í„´)
```javascript

  onLongPress={() => showActionSheet(item)}
  activeOpacity={0.7}
>
  {/* Card content */}
</TouchableOpacity>

  Alert.alert('ì œëª©', 'ë©”ì‹œì§€', [
    { text: 'ì·¨ì†Œ', style: 'cancel' },
    { text: 'ìˆ˜ì •', onPress: () => handleEdit(item) },
    { text: 'ì‚­ì œ', style: 'destructive', onPress: () => handleDelete(item.id) }
  ]);
};
```

### 4. Ownership Check Pattern (ì†Œìœ ê¶Œ í™•ì¸ íŒ¨í„´)
```javascript
// í˜„ì¬ ì‚¬ìš©ì ë¡œë“œ
const [currentUser, setCurrentUser] = useState(null);

useEffect(() => {
  loadCurrentUser();
}, []);

// ë³¸ì¸ í™•ì¸ í›„ ë²„íŠ¼ í‘œì‹œ
{currentUser && currentUser.id === item.userId && (
  <View style={styles.actions}>
    <TouchableOpacity onPress={() => handleEdit(item)}>
      <Icon name="edit" />
    </TouchableOpacity>
    <TouchableOpacity onPress={() => handleDelete(item.id)}>
      <Icon name="delete" />
    </TouchableOpacity>
  </View>
)}
```

```javascript
// Community grid layout
<View style={styles.communitiesGrid}>
  {userCommunities.map(item => {
    const community = item.community || item;
    const communityName = community.name || 'ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹°';
    const communityLocation = community.location || 'ìœ„ì¹˜ ë¯¸ì •';
    const communitySchedule = community.schedule || '';
    const communityImage = community.imageUrl || null;
    const memberCount = community.memberCount || 0;
    const maxMembers = community.maxMembers || 0;

    return (
      <View key={item.id} style={styles.communityCard}>
        <TouchableOpacity onPress={() => router.push(`/community/${item.communityId || item.id}`)}>
          {communityImage ? (
            <Image source={{ uri: communityImage }} style={styles.communityCardImage} />
          ) : (
            <View style={[styles.communityCardImage, styles.communityImagePlaceholder]}>
              <Feather name="users" size={40} color="#cbd5e1" />
            </View>
          )}
          <View style={styles.communityCardContent}>
            <Text style={styles.communityCardTitle}>{communityName}</Text>
            <View style={styles.communityCardInfo}>
              <View style={styles.communityInfoRow}>
                <Feather name="map-pin" size={12} color="#9ca3af" />
                <Text style={styles.communityInfoText}>{communityLocation}</Text>
              </View>
              {communitySchedule && (
                <View style={styles.communityInfoRow}>
                  <Feather name="clock" size={12} color="#9ca3af" />
                  <Text style={styles.communityInfoText}>{communitySchedule}</Text>
                </View>
              )}
              <View style={styles.communityMemberBadge}>
                <Feather name="users" size={12} color="#FF7A5C" />
                <Text style={styles.communityMemberText}>{memberCount}/{maxMembers}</Text>
              </View>
            </View>
          </View>
        </TouchableOpacity>
      </View>
    );
  })}
</View>
```

### 2. DB ë§ˆì´ê·¸ë ˆì´ì…˜: ê¸°ì¡´ ë°ì´í„°ì— hobbyName ì±„ìš°ê¸°

```typescript
// 1ë‹¨ê³„: hobby_name ì»¬ëŸ¼ ì¶”ê°€

  ALTER TABLE communities
  ADD COLUMN hobby_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT ''
`);

// 2ë‹¨ê³„: hobbies í…Œì´ë¸”ì—ì„œ hobby name ê°€ì ¸ì™€ì„œ ì±„ìš°ê¸°
await db.execute(sql`
  UPDATE communities c
  INNER JOIN hobbies h ON c.hobby_id = h.id
  SET c.hobby_name = h.name
  WHERE c.hobby_name = '' OR c.hobby_name IS NULL
`);
```

**ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼**:
```
âœ… hobby_name ì»¬ëŸ¼ ì¶”ê°€ ì™„ë£Œ
âœ… ê¸°ì¡´ ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹°ì˜ hobby_name í•„ë“œ ì±„ìš°ê¸° ì™„ë£Œ (3ê°œ)

ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹°ë³„ hobby_name:
- ì°¨ë§ˆì‹¤ë¶„!: 'ì°¨ ë¬¸í™”'
- ì´ë²ˆì£¼ ì£¼ë§ ë¼ì´ë”© í•˜ì‹¤ ë¶„ êµ¬í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤: 'ìì „ê±°'
- ì£¼ë§ëª¨ì„: 'í•œë¬¸ ê³µë¶€'
```

### 3. ëª¨ë°”ì¼ ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹° ëª©ë¡ í™”ë©´ ìˆ˜ì •

**íŒŒì¼**: [mobile/app/community.js](mobile/app/community.js:151-181)

```javascript
// âœ… ìˆ˜ì •ëœ ë¡œì§
const getImageSource = () => {
  console.log('[ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹° ì´ë¯¸ì§€] hobbyName:', community.hobbyName, 'imageUrl:', community.imageUrl);

  // 1. hobbyNameìœ¼ë¡œ hobbyImagesì—ì„œ ì§ì ‘ ì°¾ê¸° (ê°€ì¥ í™•ì‹¤í•œ ë°©ë²•)
  if (community.hobbyName && hobbyImages[community.hobbyName]) {
    console.log('[ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹° ì´ë¯¸ì§€] âœ… hobbyNameìœ¼ë¡œ ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì°¾ìŒ:', community.hobbyName);
    return hobbyImages[community.hobbyName];
  }

  // 2. ì„œë²„ ì—…ë¡œë“œ ì´ë¯¸ì§€ í™•ì¸
  if (community.imageUrl?.includes('uploads') || community.imageUrl?.includes('public')) {
    const absoluteUrl = `${API_BASE_URL}${community.imageUrl}`;
    return { uri: absoluteUrl };
  }

  // 3. HTTP URL
  if (community.imageUrl?.startsWith('http')) {
    return { uri: community.imageUrl };
  }

  // 4. ê¸°ë³¸ ì´ë¯¸ì§€
  return require('../assets/hobbies/hulife_logo.png');
};
```

### 4. ëª¨ë°”ì¼ ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹° ìƒì„¸ í™”ë©´ ìˆ˜ì •

### 5. ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹° ìƒì„± API ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸

```typescript
export async function POST(request: Request) {
  // ...

  // ì·¨ë¯¸ ì •ë³´ ì¡°íšŒí•˜ì—¬ hobbyName ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
  const hobby = await db.query.hobbies.findFirst({
    where: eq(hobbies.id, hobbyId)
  })

  if (!hobby) {
    return NextResponse.json(
      { error: "ì¡´ì¬í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ” ì·¨ë¯¸ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤" },
      { status: 404 }
    )
  }

  // ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹° ìƒì„± ì‹œ hobbyName í¬í•¨
  const [newCommunity] = await db.insert(communities).values({
    id: communityId,
    name,
    hobbyId,
    hobbyName: hobby.name, // ğŸ†• ë¹„ì •ê·œí™”: ì·¨ë¯¸ ì´ë¦„ ì €ì¥
    description,
    location,
    schedule,
    maxMembers,
    imageUrl: imageUrl || "/placeholder.svg",
    leaderId: session.userId,
    memberCount: 1,
    createdAt: new Date(),
  })
}
```

### expo-image-picker base64 ì˜µì…˜
```typescript

```

```
â”‚    â”‚          â”‚       â”‚
```

### Expo SDK 54 ë³€ê²½ì‚¬í•­

- âœ… `mediaTypes: ['images']` (New API)

### 3. ë°±ì—”ë“œ API ì™„ì „ ì¬ì‘ì„±

#### ê·¼ë³¸ ì›ì¸ ë¶„ì„ ë° í•´ê²°

**ë¬¸ì œì **:
1. ì˜ëª»ëœ session import ê²½ë¡œ: `@/lib/actions/auth` â†’ `@/lib/auth/session`

4. ë¹„íš¨ìœ¨ì ì¸ ì¿¼ë¦¬: N+1 ë¬¸ì œ

**í•´ê²°ì±…**:
- `app/api/posts/[id]/comments/route.ts` íŒ¨í„´ ì—°êµ¬ ë° ì ìš©
- `inArray()` + Mapìœ¼ë¡œ íš¨ìœ¨ì ì¸ ì‚¬ìš©ì ë°ì´í„° ë³‘í•©

#### GET - ëŒ“ê¸€ ëª©ë¡ ì¡°íšŒ
```typescript

  .select()
  .from(galleryComments)
  .where(eq(galleryComments.galleryItemId, galleryItemId))
  .orderBy(desc(galleryComments.createdAt))

// íš¨ìœ¨ì ì¸ ì‚¬ìš©ì ì •ë³´ ë³‘í•©
const userIds = [...new Set(commentsData.map(c => c.userId))]
const usersData = await db
  .select({ id: users.id, name: users.name, profileImage: users.profileImage })
  .from(users)
  .where(inArray(users.id, userIds))

const userMap = new Map(usersData.map(u => [u.id, u]))
const comments = commentsData.map(comment => ({
  ...comment,
  userName: userMap.get(comment.userId)?.name || comment.userName,
  userImage: userMap.get(comment.userId)?.profileImage || comment.userImage
}))
```

#### POST - ëŒ“ê¸€ ì‘ì„±
```typescript

const user = await db.select().from(users).where(eq(users.id, session.userId)).then(results => results[0])

await db.insert(galleryComments).values({
  id: commentId,
  galleryItemId,
  userId: session.userId,
  userName: user.name,
  userImage: user.profileImage || null,
  content: content.trim(),
})
```

### 2. Custom Next.js + Socket.IO ì„œë²„

```javascript
    // ìµœê·¼ 50ê°œ ë©”ì‹œì§€ ë¡œë“œ
```

# ğŸ”— ë”¥ë§í¬ (Deep Linking) êµ¬í˜„ (2025-11-19)

## ğŸ“Œ ì‘ì—… ë°°ê²½
ì‚¬ìš©ìê°€ ì™¸ë¶€ì—ì„œ íŠ¹ì • ì•± í™”ë©´ìœ¼ë¡œ ë°”ë¡œ ì§„ì…í•  ìˆ˜ ìˆë„ë¡ Deep Linking ê¸°ëŠ¥ êµ¬í˜„. ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹° ì´ˆëŒ€ ë§í¬, ê²Œì‹œê¸€ ê³µìœ , ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ ì‘í’ˆ ë§í¬ ë“±ì„ ì§€ì›í•˜ì—¬ ì‚¬ìš©ì ê²½í—˜ í–¥ìƒ.

## âœ… êµ¬í˜„ ì™„ë£Œ ë‚´ì—­

### 1. Expo Linking ì„¤ì •

**íŒ¨í‚¤ì§€**: `expo-linking` (Expo SDK 54ì— í¬í•¨)

**URL Scheme**: `hulifeexpoapp://`

### 2. ëª¨ë°”ì¼ ì•± Deep Link í•¸ë“¤ëŸ¬

**íŒŒì¼**: [mobile/app/_layout.js](mobile/app/_layout.js:70-125)

#### setupDeepLinking í•¨ìˆ˜ (Lines 70-92)
```javascript
const setupDeepLinking = async () => {
  try {
    // ì•±ì´ ë”¥ë§í¬ë¡œ ì—´ë ¸ì„ ë•Œ ì´ˆê¸° URL ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
    const initialUrl = await Linking.getInitialURL();
    if (initialUrl) {
      console.log('[App] ğŸ”— ì´ˆê¸° ë”¥ë§í¬ ê°ì§€:', initialUrl);
      handleDeepLink(initialUrl);
    }

    // ì•±ì´ ì‹¤í–‰ ì¤‘ì¼ ë•Œ ë”¥ë§í¬ ìˆ˜ì‹  ë¦¬ìŠ¤ë„ˆ ì„¤ì •
    const subscription = Linking.addEventListener('url', ({ url }) => {
      console.log('[App] ğŸ”— ë”¥ë§í¬ ìˆ˜ì‹ :', url);
      handleDeepLink(url);
    });

    return () => {
      subscription.remove();
    };
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[App] âŒ ë”¥ë§í¬ ì„¤ì • ì˜¤ë¥˜:', error);
  }
};
```

**í•µì‹¬ ê¸°ëŠ¥**:
- `Linking.getInitialURL()` - ì•±ì´ ë‹«íŒ ìƒíƒœì—ì„œ ë”¥ë§í¬ë¡œ ì‹¤í–‰ëœ ê²½ìš° ì´ˆê¸° URL ê°ì§€
- `Linking.addEventListener('url')` - ì•±ì´ ì‹¤í–‰ ì¤‘ì¼ ë•Œ ìƒˆ ë”¥ë§í¬ ìˆ˜ì‹ 
- ì—ëŸ¬ ì²˜ë¦¬ ë° ë¡œê¹…

#### handleDeepLink í•¨ìˆ˜ (Lines 94-125)
```javascript
const handleDeepLink = (url) => {
  try {
    // URL íŒŒì‹±: hulifeexpoapp://community/123 í˜•íƒœ
    const { hostname, path, queryParams } = Linking.parse(url);
    console.log('[App] ğŸ” ë”¥ë§í¬ íŒŒì‹±:', { hostname, path, queryParams });

    // í˜¸ìŠ¤íŠ¸ë„¤ì„ì— ë”°ë¼ ë¼ìš°íŒ…
    if (hostname === 'community' && path) {
      // ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹° ì´ˆëŒ€ ë§í¬: hulifeexpoapp://community/[id]
      router.push(`/community/${path}`);
    } else if (hostname === 'chat' && path) {
      // ì±„íŒ…ë°© ë§í¬: hulifeexpoapp://chat/[id]
      router.push(`/community/chat/${path}`);
    } else if (hostname === 'hobby' && path) {
      // ì·¨ë¯¸ ìƒì„¸ ë§í¬: hulifeexpoapp://hobby/[id]
      router.push(`/hobbies/${path}`);
    } else if (hostname === 'gallery' && path) {
      // ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ ì‘í’ˆ ë§í¬: hulifeexpoapp://gallery/[id]
      router.push(`/gallery/${path}`);
    } else if (hostname === 'post' && path) {
      // ê²Œì‹œê¸€ ë§í¬: hulifeexpoapp://post/[id]
      router.push(`/community/posts/${path}`);
    } else if (queryParams?.screen) {
      // ì¿¼ë¦¬ íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„°ë¡œ í™”ë©´ ì§€ì •: hulifeexpoapp://open?screen=/dashboard
      router.push(queryParams.screen);
    } else {
      console.log('[App] âš ï¸ ì•Œ ìˆ˜ ì—†ëŠ” ë”¥ë§í¬ í˜•ì‹:', url);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[App] âŒ ë”¥ë§í¬ ì²˜ë¦¬ ì˜¤ë¥˜:', error);
  }
};
```

**ì§€ì›í•˜ëŠ” ë”¥ë§í¬ í˜•ì‹**:
1. `hulifeexpoapp://community/[id]` - ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹° ìƒì„¸
2. `hulifeexpoapp://chat/[id]` - ì±„íŒ…ë°©
3. `hulifeexpoapp://hobby/[id]` - ì·¨ë¯¸ ìƒì„¸
4. `hulifeexpoapp://gallery/[id]` - ê°¤ëŸ¬ë¦¬ ì‘í’ˆ
5. `hulifeexpoapp://post/[id]` - ê²Œì‹œê¸€ ìƒì„¸
6. `hulifeexpoapp://open?screen=/dashboard` - ì¿¼ë¦¬ íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„° ê¸°ë°˜ ë¼ìš°íŒ…

#### Android Intent Filters (Lines 28-43)

## ğŸ” ë³´ì•ˆ ê³ ë ¤ì‚¬í•­

### 1. ì…ë ¥ ê²€ì¦
í˜„ì¬ êµ¬í˜„ì€ `path` ê°’ì„ ê·¸ëŒ€ë¡œ ì‚¬ìš©. í–¥í›„ ì¶”ê°€ ê²€ì¦ í•„ìš”:
```javascript

  const { hostname, path } = Linking.parse(url);
  
  // ID í˜•ì‹ ê²€ì¦ (UUID)
  const uuidRegex = /^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{12}$/i;
  if (!uuidRegex.test(path)) {
    console.error('[App] âŒ ì˜ëª»ëœ ID í˜•ì‹:', path);
    return;
  }

};
```
